  <raw>Mixed Open Seen For Japan Market



(RTTNews) - A cautious open is expected for Japan's market on Tuesday, as traders remain wary of the strengthening yen, weakening dollar and modest gains overnight on Wall Street. U.S. markets reversed early losses to finish in the black on the one year anniversary of the collapse of financial giant Lehman Brothers.

Japan's market moved lower on relatively light trading volume on Monday, pushed by fears that a strengthening yen will hurt the exporters.
The benchmark Nikkei 225 Average declined 242.27 points or 2.32 percent to close at 10.202.06.
Among the Nikkei component stocks, there were 15 closing higher, 207 were lower and 3 finished unchanged.
The broader Topix index was down 16.4 points or 1.7 percent at 934.05.
Among the major exporters, auto maker Honda fell 85 yen or 2.97 percent, rival Toyota Motor was down 100 yen or 2.60 percent, tire maker Bridgestone was down 55 yen or 3.30 percent, Canon was down 120 yen or 3.30 percent and Subaru maker Fuji Heavy was down 21 yen or 5.50 percent.
Japan Airlines shares rose 13 yen or 7.98 percent on reports that both American Airlines and Delta Airlines were in talks to acquire a share of JAL.
Among the steel makers, Nippon Steel dropped 9 yen or 2.59 percent, JFE Holdings was down 10 yen or 0.31 percent, Sumitomo Metal Industries was down 4 yen or 1.73 percent and Kobe Steel fell 3 yen or 1.79 percent.
In the financial sector, Mitsubishi UFJ Financial was down 9 yen or 1.65 percent, Mizuho Financial was down 4 yen or 1.96 percent, Sumitomo Mitsui was down 50 yen or 1.35 percent and Resona Holdings shed 24 yen or 1.92 percent.
In overseas trading, U.S. stocks spent much of Monday's session on the down side, with traders concerned about a budding trade tariff dispute between the U.S. and China.
Stocks turned positive in the final hour of trading however, and managed a higher close.
At the closing bell on Wall Street, the Dow Jones Industrial Average was up 21.39 points or 0.22 percent at 9.626.80, the Nasdaq Composite was up 10.88points or 0.52 percent at 2,091.78 and the Standard &amp; Poor's 500 index was up 6.61 points or 0.63 percent at 1,049.34.
Nearly all of the major Asia/Pacific region markets closed lower on Monday.
Hong Kong's Hang Seng index dropped 229.22 points or 1.08 percent to 20.932.20.
China's Shanghai Composite index managed a gain of 36.95 points or 1.24 percent to close at 3.026.74.
In India, the BSE/SENSEX index was down 50.11 points or 0.31 percent at 16,214.19.
Indonesia's Jakarta Composite index declined 33.24 points or 1.38 percent to 2.382.70.
The KOSPI/Seoul Composite index in South Korea was down 16.79 points or 1.02 percent at 1,634.91.
The Taiwan Weighted Index fell 80.19 points or 1.09 percent to 7,256.95.
For comments and feedback: contact editorial@rttnews.com
Copyright(c) 2009 RTTNews.com, Inc. All Rights Reserved</raw>
